    SELECT [o0].[Id], [o0].[OrderId], [o0].[Price], [o0].[ProductId], [o0].[Quantity], [p].[Id] AS [Id0], [p].[CategoryId], [p].[Description], [p].[ImageUrl], [p].[Name], [p].[Price] AS [Price0], [p].[Stock], [c0].[Id] AS [Id1], [c0].[Description] AS [Description0], [c0].[Name] AS [Name0]
    FROM [OrderItems] AS [o0]
    INNER JOIN [Products] AS [p] ON [o0].[ProductId] = [p].[Id]
